***vat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a> (2907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fatą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaten.html>vaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaatje.html>vaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>barrel, tank</li>

***vatten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vatten.html>vatten</a> (7835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaten.html>vaten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaten.html>vaten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*faton</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fatōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. The short <i>a</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> introduced by analogy with the uninflected singular form of the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vatten.html>vatten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grasp</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grasp mentally, to understand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch, to apprehend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch, to be afflicted with <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a disease</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vechten.html>vechten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fehtan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fehtaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peḱ-</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veearts.html>veearts</a> (22681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vee.html>vee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cattle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-iater, medical doctor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">veghe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">veyghe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">veych</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">doomed to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a>; near death</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*faigijaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fey, doomed to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*PAik-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*PAig-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ill-meaning, bad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fey</i>.

***veel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> (114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:filo.html>filo</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*felu</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>many, much, a lot of</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>As a determiner <i><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></i> typically isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> inflected in informal Dutch. In formal style the inflected form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a></i> may be used, but only for plurals or before (usually uncountable) singular nouns with a definite article:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>Vele</a></b> rolstoelgebruikers <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezwaren.html>bezwaren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plannen.html>plannen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Many</b> wheelchair users <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> objections against the plans.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweld.html>geweld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dreef.html>dreef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inwoners.html>inwoners</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>large amount</b> of violence drove inhabitants away.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>

***veelvraat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veelvraat.html>veelvraat</a> (31498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1710; compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">much</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vraat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gobbling, eating gluttonously</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vielfraß</i> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Veelfraat</i>. The term originally meant simply ‘glutton’ in German, but <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> applied to the <a href = vnd.unilang:hyena.html>hyena</a> in pre-modern times. In the 15th century, Old <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">fjellfross</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mountain cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed into Middle Low German by Hanseatic fur traders as <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">villevrās</i> and folk-etymologically blended with the existing word for ‘glutton’, possibly influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi">ahma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glutton; <a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, giving <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">veelvratz</i> (Reinke <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>Vos</a>, 1498), <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">vēlevrās</i>, <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">vēlevrāt</i>. The meaning ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a>’ <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> initially the only one received into Dutch, although by 1849 the word <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> acquired the meaning ‘glutton’.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veelvraat.html>veelvraat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veelvraten.html>veelvraten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veelvraat.html>veelvraatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>glutton
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slokop.html>slokop</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vraat</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a>, <i>Gulo gulo</i></li></ol>

***veer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veer.html>veer</a> (10301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">veder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vedere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fethara</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*feþrō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*péth₂r̥ ~ pth₂én-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feather, wing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peth₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense "spring" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from the ability of <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> to resume their shape when <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Fedder</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Feder</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fear</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">feather</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">fjer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">fjäder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veer.html>veer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veren.html>veren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veertje.html>veertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>feather
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluim.html>pluim</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>spring (e.g. metallic helix which resists stress)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="4" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bladveer</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">dinosaurusveer</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:veren.html>vere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">feri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*farją</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fähre</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veerkracht.html>veerkracht</a> (46225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***veertig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veertig.html>veertig</a> (3060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">viertich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vēertich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*viertig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fedwōr tigiwiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veertig.html>veertig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>forty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">v-</i>, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally pronounced with initial <span class="IPA">/f/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in accents that generally do not devoice <i>v-</i>. (This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeventig.html>zeventig</a></i> ["seventy"], which used to have a prefix <i>t-</i> and hence a devoiced <i>z-</i>.) However, there are also many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> who pronounce <span class="IPA">/v/</span> in line with the spelling. The WNT (1954) notes that the voiced pronunciation isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> very common, while Auer and Hinskens state that this realisation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> becoming increasingly common in Standard Dutch due to hypercorrection.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a> (17435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>vegetarian (relating to the type of diet eaten by vegetarians)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>While <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vegetariër</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the standard noun to refer to someone who follows a vegetarian diet, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also not uncommonly used to refer to people. Thus, "<a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a>?" (<i>are you vegetarian?</i>) might be used to ask someone if they eat a vegetarian diet instead of the more standard "<a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> vegetariër?" (<i>are you a vegetarian?</i>). However, since <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></i> in standard Dutch refers only to food and not to the people who follow a vegetarian diet, this usage of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></i> to refer to people <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often considered incorrect.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> vegetariërs
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> at <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:restaurant.html>restaurant</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>vegetariër, vegetarisme, fruitarisch, <a href = vnd.unilang:vega.html>vega</a></li></ul>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
</body>

***veilig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veilig.html>veilig</a> (524)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">veilich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*failijaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">true, familiar, good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Note the conflation of the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> with <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*faliz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">venal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in cognates <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veilen.html>veil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">venal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">feil</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">venal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***vel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a> (6761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:fel.html>fel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fellą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pello-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pelno-</i>, whence Latin pellis, Greek πέλλα; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fell</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vellen.html>vellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:velletje.html>velletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A skin, a hide.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>Haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:velletje.html>velletje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Her <b>skin</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> caught in the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A fur, a pelt.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tientallen.html>Tientallen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vellen.html>vellen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beren.html>beren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wolven.html>wolven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lagen.html>lagen</a> opeengestapeld.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Tens of <b>pelts</b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:bears.html>bears</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:wolves.html>wolves</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> stacked on each other.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A sheet (e.g. of paper; incorrectly used for a page).
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:glas.html>glas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gloeilamp.html>gloeilamp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dikker.html>dikker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>The glass of a lightbulb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not much thicker than a </i>sheet<i> of paper.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>A membrane, e.g. forming on boiling milk.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saus.html>saus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koken.html>koken</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstaan.html>ontstaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vellen.html>vellen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This sauce shouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> boil for too long or else <b>membranes</b> will appear.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A rag, a shred.</li></ol>

***veldslag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veldslag.html>veldslag</a> (12263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veld.html>veld</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">field</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">battle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Feldschlacht</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veldslag.html>veldslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veldslagen.html>veldslagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veldslag.html>veldslagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">battle</span> on open <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">therefore excluding sieges</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">veltslach</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veld.html>veld</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veldslag.html>veldslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veldslagen.html>veldslagen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The practice of letting livestock <a href = vnd.unilang:grazen.html>graze</a> on the commons. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vēlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*felan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*felhaną</i>.

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>As for all adjectives that can also be used as pronouns, the plural ending <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">(e)n</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only used when referring to people. For animals or inanimate <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, if inflected at all, a plural ending <i>-e</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used.
</p>

***velociraptor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:velociraptor.html>velociraptor</a> (78583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mul"><a href = vnd.unilang:velociraptor.html>Velociraptor</a></i> genus name, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vēlōx</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:raptor.html>raptor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thief</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:velociraptor.html>velociraptor</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">velociraptors</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small agile dinosaur, of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:velociraptor.html>Velociraptor</a></i>, having sickle-shaped claws. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also thought to have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a feathered coat. Fossils have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> found in Late Cretaceous deposits Mongolia and China (around 75-71 mya)</li></ol>
</body>

***ven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ven.html>ven</a> (46224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">venne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*feni</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fanją</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veen.html>veen</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:venster.html>venster</a></i> (<span class="Latn" lang="dum">venstre</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="dum">veinster</span>, etc.), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fenstar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fenestra</i>. ***vent.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a> (496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hero; <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Unknown earlier origin. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">feint</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">servant; fellow; boyfriend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Fent</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young fellow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<ul><li>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*fanþijō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">walker, walking</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pent-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go, pass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This would make it related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to find; (archaic) to explore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fendo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">footsoldier</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fēþa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">footsoldier</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The expected descendant in Dutch would have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <i>vend(e)</i>, which existed in Middle Dutch as <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vende</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pawn in a chess game; farmer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Final_obstruent_devoicing" class="extiw" title="w:Final obstruent devoicing">Final-obstruent devoicing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common in Dutch and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already widespread in Old Dutch, rendering <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a></i> as a variant of <i>vend(e)</i> possible.</li>
<li>Possibly a shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vennoot.html>vennoot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">partner (in a company)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> equivalent to a compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">veem</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(storage) company</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:genoot.html>genoot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">companion, partner</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no evidence of an overlap in senses.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:venten.html>venten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ventje.html>ventje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chap, fellow</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
